## 70. Oct 9, 2025 Â· 9:40 AM UTC Â· 1976221330186846233#m
- é“¾æŽ¥ï¼šhttps://twitter.com/yuyue_chris/status/1976221330186846233#m

> A recap on how I aped BNBHolders at 300k
>  
> Yesterday I saw so many ppl talking about the new memelauch pad on binance alpha wallet, where the 1mil bonding curved can only be filled through binance alpha wallet. So I get myself prepared, pre-adjusted the gas and slippage cuz I reckon the first one will be filled instantly. Also I was afraid there could be some max wallet limit cuz I only have one keyless wallet. Thank god there's no max wallet
>  
> Since the past few days I reckon all the bsc runners were from asian time. Binance team based in UAE so I reckon 6am UTC to 6PM UTC could be the launching window since both ppl from China and UAE are up. I based in Germany so I woke up at 7am, saw @heyibinance post something to warm up. By that time I have a very strong feeling it's coming
>  
> During the waiting time I told my family @0xTheBigBlue to get ready, gave the info about 1mil bonding curve while ppl was so confused why so many traders been buying T4, which is obvious the wrong one cuz it filled at 70k, not 1mil. I only trust onchain stuff, plus the bottom fillers so I walked away from this coin. S from bigblue found this token on chain, which cant be bought but has a 1mil bonding curve, created from fourmeme router, starts with 0x4444, which gave me a very strong feeling the 1mil curve should start with 0x4444. This helped me a lot when I saw the BNBHolder popped out from memerush. Then I aped 5 +5 bnb at the bonding curve.
>  
> Feel free to dd on this test token, it cannot be aped so no worry for another pvp
>  
> 0x4444ce1d7f81a5756e1adf4df562b3163de2e0ae
